Local Open Scope cat.

Section IsoInserters.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {b₁ b₂ : B}
          {f g : b₁ --> b₂}.

  (**
   1. Cones
   *)
  Definition iso_inserter_cone
    : UU
    := ∑ (i : B)
         (m : i --> b₁),
       invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g).

  Definition make_iso_inserter_cone
             (i : B)
             (m : i --> b₁)
             (α : invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g))
    : iso_inserter_cone
    := i ,, m ,, α.

  Coercion iso_inserter_cone_ob
           (cone : iso_inserter_cone)
    : B
    := pr1 cone.

  Definition iso_inserter_cone_pr1
             (cone : iso_inserter_cone)
    : cone --> b₁
    := pr12 cone.

  Definition iso_inserter_cone_cell
             (cone : iso_inserter_cone)
    : invertible_2cell
        (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone · f)
        (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone · g)
    := pr22 cone.

  Definition iso_inserter_1cell
             (cone₁ cone₂ : iso_inserter_cone)
    : UU
    := ∑ (k : cone₁ --> cone₂)
         (α : invertible_2cell
                (k · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
                (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)),
       (k ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
       • lassociator _ _ _
       • (α ▹ g)
       =
       lassociator _ _ _
       • (α ▹ f)
       • iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₁.

  Definition make_iso_inserter_1cell
             {cone₁ cone₂ : iso_inserter_cone}
             (k : cone₁ --> cone₂)
             (α : invertible_2cell
                    (k · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
                    (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁))
             (p : (k ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
                  • lassociator _ _ _
                  • (α ▹ g)
                  =
                  lassociator _ _ _
                  • (α ▹ f)
                  • iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₁)
    : iso_inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂
    := k ,, α ,, p.

  Coercion iso_inserter_1cell_mor
           {cone₁ cone₂ : iso_inserter_cone}
           (u : iso_inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂)
    : cone₁ --> cone₂
    := pr1 u.

  Definition iso_inserter_1cell_pr1
             {cone₁ cone₂ : iso_inserter_cone}
             (u : iso_inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂)
    : invertible_2cell
        (u · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
        (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)
    := pr12 u.

  Definition iso_inserter_1cell_cell
             {cone₁ cone₂ : iso_inserter_cone}
             (u : iso_inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂)
    : (_ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
       • lassociator _ _ _
       • (iso_inserter_1cell_pr1 u ▹ g)
       =
       lassociator _ _ _
       • (iso_inserter_1cell_pr1 u ▹ f)
       • iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₁
    := pr22 u.

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone₁, cone₂: iso_inserter_cone
φ, ψ: iso_inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂
p₁: pr1 φ = pr1 ψ
p₂: pr112 φ =
(idtoiso_2_1 (pr1 φ) (pr1 ψ) p₁
 ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) • pr112 ψ
φ = ψ

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone₁, cone₂: iso_inserter_cone
φ, ψ: iso_inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂
p₁: pr1 φ = pr1 ψ
p₂: pr112 φ =
(idtoiso_2_1 (pr1 φ) (pr1 ψ) p₁
 ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) • pr112 ψ
φ = ψ

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone₁, cone₂: iso_inserter_cone
φ₁: B ⟦ cone₁, cone₂ ⟧
φ₂: invertible_2cell
  (φ₁ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
  (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)
φ₃: ((φ₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
 • lassociator φ₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) g)
• (φ₂ ▹ g) =
(lassociator φ₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) f
 • (φ₂ ▹ f)) • iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₁
ψ: iso_inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂
p₁: pr1 (φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃) = pr1 ψ
p₂: pr112 (φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃) =
(idtoiso_2_1 (pr1 (φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃)) (pr1 ψ) p₁
 ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) • pr112 ψ
φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃ = ψ

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone₁, cone₂: iso_inserter_cone
φ₁: B ⟦ cone₁, cone₂ ⟧
φ₂: invertible_2cell
  (φ₁ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
  (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)
φ₃: ((φ₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
 • lassociator φ₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) g)
• (φ₂ ▹ g) =
(lassociator φ₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) f
 • (φ₂ ▹ f)) • iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₁
ψ₁: B ⟦ cone₁, cone₂ ⟧
ψ₂: invertible_2cell
  (ψ₁ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
  (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)
ψ₃: ((ψ₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
 • lassociator ψ₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) g)
• (ψ₂ ▹ g) =
(lassociator ψ₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) f
 • (ψ₂ ▹ f)) • iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₁
p₁: pr1 (φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃) = pr1 (ψ₁,, ψ₂,, ψ₃)
p₂: pr112 (φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃) =
(idtoiso_2_1 (pr1 (φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃))
   (pr1 (ψ₁,, ψ₂,, ψ₃)) p₁
 ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
• pr112 (ψ₁,, ψ₂,, ψ₃)
φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃ = ψ₁,, ψ₂,, ψ₃

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone₁, cone₂: iso_inserter_cone

  (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)

 • (ψ₂ ▹ f)) • iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₁

(idtoiso_2_1 φ₁ ψ₁ p₁
 ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) • 
pr1 ψ₂
φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃ = ψ₁,, ψ₂,, ψ₃

(lassociator φ₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) f
 • (ψ₂ ▹ f)) • iso_inserter_cone_cell cone₁
p₂: pr1 φ₂ =
(idtoiso_2_1 φ₁ φ₁ (idpath φ₁)
 ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) • 
pr1 ψ₂
isPredicate is_invertible_2cell

  (**
   2. The universal mapping property
   *)
  Section UniversalMappingProperty.
    Context (cone : iso_inserter_cone).

    Definition has_iso_inserter_ump_1
      : UU
      := ∏ (other_cone : iso_inserter_cone),
         iso_inserter_1cell other_cone cone.

    Definition has_iso_inserter_ump_2
      : UU
      := ∏ (x : B)
           (u₁ u₂ : x --> cone)
           (α : u₁ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone
                ==>
                u₂ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
           (p : rassociator _ _ _
                • (u₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone)
                • lassociator _ _ _
                • (α ▹ g)
                =
                (α ▹ f)
                • rassociator _ _ _
                • (u₂ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone)
                • lassociator _ _ _),
         ∑ (ζ : u₁ ==> u₂),
         ζ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α.

    Definition has_iso_inserter_ump_eq
      : UU
      := ∏ (x : B)
           (u₁ u₂ : x --> cone)
           (α : u₁ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone
                ==>
                u₂ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
           (p : rassociator _ _ _
                • (u₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone)
                • lassociator _ _ _
                • (α ▹ g)
                =
                (α ▹ f)
                • rassociator _ _ _
                • (u₂ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone)
                • lassociator _ _ _)
           (φ₁ φ₂ : u₁ ==> u₂)
           (q₁ : φ₁ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α)
           (q₂ : φ₂ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α),
         φ₁ = φ₂.

    Definition has_iso_inserter_ump
      : UU
      := has_iso_inserter_ump_1 × has_iso_inserter_ump_2 × has_iso_inserter_ump_eq.
  End UniversalMappingProperty.

  Section Projections.
    Context {cone : iso_inserter_cone}
            (H : has_iso_inserter_ump cone).

    Definition iso_inserter_ump_mor
               {i : B}
               (m : i --> b₁)
               (α : invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g))
      : i --> cone
      := pr1 H (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α).

    Definition iso_inserter_ump_mor_pr1
               {i : B}
               (m : i --> b₁)
               (α : invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g))
      : invertible_2cell
          (iso_inserter_ump_mor m α · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
          m
      := iso_inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 H (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)).

    Definition iso_inserter_ump_mor_cell
               {i : B}
               (m : i --> b₁)
               (α : invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g))
      : (_ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone)
        • lassociator _ _ _
        • (iso_inserter_ump_mor_pr1 m α ▹ g)
        =
        lassociator _ _ _
        • (iso_inserter_ump_mor_pr1 m α ▹ f)
        • α
      := iso_inserter_1cell_cell (pr1 H (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)).

    Definition iso_inserter_ump_cell
               {x : B}
               {u₁ u₂ : x --> cone}
               (α : u₁ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone
                    ==>
                    u₂ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
               (p : rassociator _ _ _
                    • (u₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone)
                    • lassociator _ _ _
                    • (α ▹ g)
                    =
                    (α ▹ f)
                    • rassociator _ _ _
                    • (u₂ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone)
                    • lassociator _ _ _)
      : u₁ ==> u₂
      := pr1 (pr12 H x u₁ u₂ α p).

    Definition iso_inserter_ump_cell_pr1
               {x : B}
               {u₁ u₂ : x --> cone}
               (α : u₁ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone
                    ==>
                    u₂ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
               (p : rassociator _ _ _
                    • (u₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone)
                    • lassociator _ _ _
                    • (α ▹ g)
                    =
                    (α ▹ f)
                    • rassociator _ _ _
                    • (u₂ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone)
                    • lassociator _ _ _)
      : iso_inserter_ump_cell α p ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α
      := pr2 (pr12 H x u₁ u₂ α p).

    Definition iso_inserter_ump_eq
               {x : B}
               {u₁ u₂ : x --> cone}
               (α : u₁ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone
                    ==>
                    u₂ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
               (p : rassociator _ _ _
                    • (u₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone)
                    • lassociator _ _ _
                    • (α ▹ g)
                    =
                    (α ▹ f)
                    • rassociator _ _ _
                    • (u₂ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone)
                    • lassociator _ _ _)
               (φ₁ φ₂ : u₁ ==> u₂)
               (q₁ : φ₁ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α)
               (q₂ : φ₂ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α)
      : φ₁ = φ₂
      := pr22 H x u₁ u₂ α p φ₁ φ₂ q₁ q₂.

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone: iso_inserter_cone
H: has_iso_inserter_ump cone
x: B

φ₁, φ₂: u₁ ==> u₂
p: ((rassociator u₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f
  • (u₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))

• ((φ₁ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ g) =
((((φ₁ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ f)
  • rassociator u₂ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
 • (u₂ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
• lassociator u₂ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g
q: φ₁ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone =
φ₂ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone
φ₁ = φ₂

φ₁, φ₂: u₁ ==> u₂
p: ((rassociator u₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f
  • (u₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
 • lassociator u₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g)
• ((φ₁ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ g) =
((((φ₁ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ f)
  • rassociator u₂ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
 • (u₂ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
• lassociator u₂ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g
q: φ₁ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone =
φ₂ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone
φ₁ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone =
φ₁ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone
 apply idpath.

q: φ₁ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone =

 exact (!q).
    Qed.
  End Projections.

  Section Invertible2CellIso_inserterUMP.
    Context {cone : iso_inserter_cone}
            (H : has_iso_inserter_ump cone)
            {x : B}
            {u₁ u₂ : x --> cone}
            (α : u₁ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone
                 ==>
                 u₂ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
            (p : rassociator _ _ _
                 • (u₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone)
                 • lassociator _ _ _
                 • (α ▹ g)
                 =
                 (α ▹ f)
                 • rassociator _ _ _
                 • (u₂ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone)
                 • lassociator _ _ _)
            (Hα : is_invertible_2cell α).

inv:= iso_inserter_ump_cell H Hα ^-1
  is_invertible_2cell_iso_inserter_ump_cell_inv_path: u₂ ==> u₁
(((rassociator u₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f
   • (u₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
  • lassociator u₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g)
 • ((iso_inserter_ump_cell H α p
     ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ g))
• ((iso_inserter_ump_cell H Hα ^-1
      is_invertible_2cell_iso_inserter_ump_cell_inv_path
    ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ g) =
(((((iso_inserter_ump_cell H α p
     ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ f)
   • ((iso_inserter_ump_cell H Hα ^-1
         is_invertible_2cell_iso_inserter_ump_cell_inv_path
       ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ f))
  • rassociator u₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
 • (u₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
• lassociator u₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g

  (iso_inserter_ump_cell χ₁
     (iso_inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q)

         · g ==>
         pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q) · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone
         · g)

         • ((iso_inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)) ^-1
            ▹ g))
        (λ p : pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q)
               · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone · g ==>
               pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)
               · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone · g,
         ((rassociator (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q))
             (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f
           • (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q)
              ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
          • lassociator (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q))
              (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g) • p =
         ((((iso_inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q)
             • (iso_inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)) ^-1)
            ▹ f)
           • rassociator (pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q))
               (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
          • (pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)
             ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
         • lassociator (pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q))
             (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g)
        (internal_paths_rew
           (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q)
            · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone · f ==>
            pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)
            · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone · f)

            • ((iso_inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)) ^-1
               ▹ f))
           (λ p : pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q)
                  · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone · f ==>
                  pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)
                  · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone · f,
            ((rassociator (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q))
                (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f
              • (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q)
                 ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
             • lassociator (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q))
                 (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g)

                  ^-1 ▹ g)) =

              • rassociator (pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q))
                  (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
             • (pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)
                ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))

                (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g)
           (internal_paths_rew_r

               pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)

                • (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q)

• (φ ▹ g) =
(((φ ▹ f)
  • rassociator u₂ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
 • (u₂ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
• lassociator u₂ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g
u₁ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone ==>
u₂ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone
 exact φ.

        apply cellset_property.
  Qed.

x: B

  (λ f0 : hom x cone ⟦ u₁, u₂ ⟧,
   # (iso_inserter_cone_functor cone x) f0) α
p: ((rassociator u₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f
  • (u₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
 • lassociator u₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g)
• (pr1 α ▹ g) =
(((pr1 α ▹ f)
  • rassociator u₂ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
 • (u₂ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
• lassociator u₂ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g
((rassociator u₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f
  • (u₁ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
 • lassociator u₁ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g)
• ((pr1 φ₁ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ g) =
((((pr1 φ₁ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ f)
  • rassociator u₂ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
 • (u₂ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
• lassociator u₂ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g

B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
cone: iso_inserter_cone
H: has_iso_inserter_ump cone
x: B
h: cat_iso_inserter (post_comp x f) (post_comp x g)
is_z_isomorphism
  (pr1
     (((let X :=
          λ (H : has_iso_inserter_ump cone) (i : B)
          (m : B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧)
          (α : invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)),
          pr1 (iso_inserter_ump_mor_pr1 H m α) in
        X H x (pr1 h) (pr2 h))
       :
       hom x b₁
       ⟦ pr1
           (iso_inserter_cone_functor cone x
              (iso_inserter_ump_mor H (pr1 h) (pr2 h))),
       pr1 h ⟧),,
      (make_is_universal_iso_inserter_cone_essentially_surjective_subproof
         h
       :
       (λ f0 : hom x b₁
               ⟦ pr1
                   (iso_inserter_cone_functor cone x
                      (iso_inserter_ump_mor H (pr1 h)
                         (pr2 h))), pr1 h ⟧,
        Core.mor_disp
          (pr2
             (iso_inserter_cone_functor cone x
                (iso_inserter_ump_mor H (pr1 h)
                   (pr2 h)))) (pr2 h) f0)
         ((let X :=
             λ (H : has_iso_inserter_ump cone) (i : B)
             (m : B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧)
             (α : invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)),
             pr1 (iso_inserter_ump_mor_pr1 H m α) in
           X H x (pr1 h) (pr2 h))
          :
          hom x b₁
          ⟦ pr1
              (iso_inserter_cone_functor cone x
                 (iso_inserter_ump_mor H (pr1 h)
                    (pr2 h))), pr1 h ⟧))))
 
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B

x: B
h: cat_iso_inserter (post_comp x f) (post_comp x g)
is_invertible_2cell
  (pr1
     (((let X :=
          λ (H : has_iso_inserter_ump cone) (i : B)
          (m : B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧)
          (α : invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)),
          pr1 (iso_inserter_ump_mor_pr1 H m α) in
        X H x (pr1 h) (pr2 h))
       :
       hom x b₁
       ⟦ pr1
           (iso_inserter_cone_functor cone x
              (iso_inserter_ump_mor H (pr1 h) (pr2 h))),
       pr1 h ⟧),,
      (make_is_universal_iso_inserter_cone_essentially_surjective_subproof
         h
       :
       (λ f0 : hom x b₁
               ⟦ pr1
                   (iso_inserter_cone_functor cone x
                      (iso_inserter_ump_mor H (pr1 h)
                         (pr2 h))), pr1 h ⟧,
        Core.mor_disp
          (pr2
             (iso_inserter_cone_functor cone x
                (iso_inserter_ump_mor H (pr1 h)
                   (pr2 h)))) (pr2 h) f0)
         ((let X :=
             λ (H : has_iso_inserter_ump cone) (i : B)
             (m : B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧)
             (α : invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)),
             pr1 (iso_inserter_ump_mor_pr1 H m α) in
           X H x (pr1 h) (pr2 h))
          :
          hom x b₁
          ⟦ pr1
              (iso_inserter_cone_functor cone x
                 (iso_inserter_ump_mor H (pr1 h)
                    (pr2 h))), pr1 h ⟧))))

          apply property_from_invertible_2cell.
    Defined.
  End MakeUniversalIso_inserterCone.

        := iso_inserter_cone_pr1 q ,, iso_inserter_cone_cell q.

        : q --> cone
        := right_adjoint (H q) alg.

  (λ x0 : u₁ · iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone ==>

   (x0 ▹ f)

       • (u₂ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
      • lassociator u₂ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g))

(((α ▹ f)

 • (u₂ ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell cone))
• lassociator u₂ (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g

     u₂ φ₁) =
pr1
  ((φ₂ ▹ iso_inserter_cone_pr1 cone),,
   iso_inserter_cone_functor_data_subproof cone x u₁
     u₂ φ₂)

Arguments iso_inserter_cone {_ _ _} _ _.

(**
 4. Bicategories with iso_inserters
 *)
Definition has_iso_inserters
           (B : bicat)
  : UU
  := ∏ (b₁ b₂ : B)
       (f g : b₁ --> b₂),
     ∑ (i : B)
       (m : i --> b₁)
       (α : invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)),
     has_iso_inserter_ump (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α).

(**
 5. Iso_inserters are faithful
 *)

B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)
H: has_iso_inserter_ump
  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
faithful_1cell m


B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)
H: has_iso_inserter_ump
  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
faithful_1cell m

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)
H: has_iso_inserter_ump
  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β₁, β₂: g₁ ==> g₂
p: β₁ ▹ m = β₂ ▹ m
β₁ = β₂

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)
H: has_iso_inserter_ump
  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β₁, β₂: g₁ ==> g₂
p: β₁ ▹ m = β₂ ▹ m
((rassociator g₁ m f • (g₁ ◃ α)) • lassociator g₁ m g)
• ((β₁ ▹ m) ▹ g) =
((((β₁ ▹ m) ▹ f) • rassociator g₂ m f) • (g₂ ◃ α))
• lassociator g₂ m g
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B

  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β₁, β₂: g₁ ==> g₂
p: β₁ ▹ m = β₂ ▹ m
β₁ ▹ m = β₂ ▹ m

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)
H: has_iso_inserter_ump
  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β₁, β₂: g₁ ==> g₂
p: β₁ ▹ m = β₂ ▹ m
((rassociator g₁ m f • (g₁ ◃ α)) • lassociator g₁ m g)
• ((β₁ ▹ m) ▹ g) =
((((β₁ ▹ m) ▹ f) • rassociator g₂ m f) • (g₂ ◃ α))
• lassociator g₂ m g
 abstract
      (rewrite rwhisker_rwhisker_alt ;
       rewrite !vassocl ;
       apply maponpaths ;
       rewrite rwhisker_rwhisker ;
       rewrite !vassocr ;
       apply maponpaths_2 ;
       refine (!_) ;
       apply vcomp_whisker).
  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧

  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)

β₁, β₂: g₁ ==> g₂
p: β₁ ▹ m = β₂ ▹ m
β₁ ▹ m = β₂ ▹ m
 exact p.

(**
 6. Iso_inserters are conservative
 *)
Section Iso_inserterConservative.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {b₁ b₂ : B}
          {f g : b₁ --> b₂}
          {i : B}
          (m : i --> b₁)
          (α : invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g))
          (H : has_iso_inserter_ump (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α))
          {x : B}
          {g₁ g₂ : x --> i}
          (β : g₁ ==> g₂)
          (Hβ : is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)).

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)
H: has_iso_inserter_ump
  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
g₂ ==> g₁

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)
H: has_iso_inserter_ump
  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
g₂ ==> g₁

b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧

  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
g₂
· iso_inserter_cone_pr1 (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α) ==>
g₁
· iso_inserter_cone_pr1 (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)
H: has_iso_inserter_ump
  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
((rassociator g₂
    (iso_inserter_cone_pr1
       (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)) f
  • (g₂
     ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell
         (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)))
 • lassociator g₂
     (iso_inserter_cone_pr1
        (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)) g) • (?α ▹ g) =
(((?α ▹ f)
  • rassociator g₁
      (iso_inserter_cone_pr1
         (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)) f)
 • (g₁
    ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell
        (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)))
• lassociator g₁
    (iso_inserter_cone_pr1
       (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)) g

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)
H: has_iso_inserter_ump
  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
g₂
· iso_inserter_cone_pr1 (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α) ==>
g₁
· iso_inserter_cone_pr1 (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
 exact Hβ^-1.
    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)
H: has_iso_inserter_ump
  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
((rassociator g₂
    (iso_inserter_cone_pr1
       (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)) f
  • (g₂
     ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell
         (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)))
 • lassociator g₂
     (iso_inserter_cone_pr1
        (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)) g)
• (Hβ ^-1 ▹ g) =
(((Hβ ^-1 ▹ f)
  • rassociator g₁
      (iso_inserter_cone_pr1
         (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)) f)
 • (g₁
    ◃ iso_inserter_cone_cell
        (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)))
• lassociator g₁
    (iso_inserter_cone_pr1
       (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)) g
 abstract
        (cbn ;
         use vcomp_move_R_Mp ; [ is_iso | ] ; cbn ;
         rewrite !vassocl ;
         rewrite rwhisker_rwhisker ;
         use vcomp_move_L_pM ; [ is_iso | ] ; cbn ;
         rewrite !vassocr ;
         apply maponpaths_2 ;
         rewrite rwhisker_rwhisker_alt ;
         rewrite !vassocl ;
         apply maponpaths ;
         rewrite vcomp_whisker ;
         apply idpath).
  Defined.

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)
H: has_iso_inserter_ump
  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)

g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
β • iso_inserter_conservative_inv = id₂ g₁

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (m · f) (m · g)
H: has_iso_inserter_ump
  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
β • iso_inserter_conservative_inv = id₂ g₁

  • rassociator g₁ m f) • (g₁ ◃ α))

g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
g₂ ==> g₁

  (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)
